    function getSyncDFPCookie(syncdfpcname) {
        var syncdfpname = syncdfpcname + '=';
        var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
        var sdca = decodedCookie.split(';');
        for(var i = 0; i < sdca.length; i++) {
            var c = sdca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                c = c.substring(1);
            }
            if (c.indexOf(syncdfpname) == 0) {
                return c.substring(syncdfpname.length, c.length);
            }
        }
        return "";
    }

	});
	 function moveFotomotoCart1010256() {
	/* get the width of the image blocks and make that the height of the image blocks */
		var bodywidth1010256 = $('body').width();
		if (bodywidth1010256 > 991) {
                    $('#tncms-block-1010256').append($('#fotomoto_view_cart_float'));
                } else {
                    $('#site-container').append($('#fotomoto_view_cart_float'));
                }
	};
        
    	$(function() {
            var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
                moveFotomotoCart1010256();
            });
            var target = document.querySelector('#fotomotoWidgetContainer');
                observer.observe(target, {
                attributes: true
            }); 
        });

         <script>
          $(document).ready(function(){
    	$('#lnp-closings').hide();
		closingsCheck();
	});
	function closingsCheck() {
        /* need to override syncSDK ajaxSetup */
		$.cachedAjaxSetup = $.extend(true, {}, $.ajaxSetup());
		$.ajaxSetup({
        	beforeSend: function (xhr) {    
        	}
        });
		$.getJSON('https://dagobah.lancasteronline.com/closings/closings-new.php/closings', function(json){
        	thehtml= "";
			if (json.response.count > 0) {
				$('#lnp-closings').show();		
			} else {
				thehtml = '';
                                $('#lnp-closings-wrapper').html(thehtml);
				$('#lnp-closings').hide();
			}
            /* need to reset ajax */
    		$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);          
            
		});
	}
         </script>

           <script>
            $(document).ready(function () {
	/* need to override syncSDK ajaxSetup */
	$.cachedAjaxSetup = $.extend(true, {}, $.ajaxSetup());
	$.ajaxSetup({
		beforeSend: function (xhr) {    
		}
	});





parsepopIDArr = [];
$.getJSON('https://api.parsely.com/v2/analytics/posts?apikey=lancasteronline.com&secret=p6qZaWT52kuVsxdJQvOIettRZdtlk89aWHYwm8GICEU&limit=10&sort=views&pub_date_start=30d&period_start=24h', 
	function(presponse){
	})
	.done(function(presponse) {
		if (presponse.success) {
			if (presponse.data.length > 0) {
				$.each(presponse.data, function(key, tmpartinfo) {
                                        if (tmpartinfo.url.includes('article_')) {
						tmpid = tmpartinfo.url.split('article_');
					} else if (tmpartinfo.url.includes('collection_')) {
						tmpid = tmpartinfo.url.split('collection_');
					} else if (tmpartinfo.url.includes('video_')) {
						tmpid = tmpartinfo.url.split('video_');
					}
					tmpida = tmpid[tmpid.length - 1].split('.html');
					
                                        if (parsepopIDArr.indexOf(tmpida[0]) == -1) {
                                            parsepopIDArr.push(tmpida[0]);
                                            if (parsepopIDArr.length <= 5) {
                                                $('#block-1002915-lnp-most-popular-list').append('<li class=""><a href="'+tmpartinfo.url+'&utm_source=general&utm_medium=list&utm_campaign=People%20Are%20Reading'+'">'+tmpartinfo.title+'<\/a><\/li>');
                                            }
                                        }
                                
					
				});
			} else {
				
					
				
				$.getJSON('https://lancasteronline.com/search/?f=json&t=article&&l=5&sort=date&c[]=news/local&k=&b=&sd=desc&d1=24%20hours%20ago&xd=1',
				function(lnpsearchlist, status) {
				})
				.done(function(lnpsearchlist) {
					$.each(lnpsearchlist.rows, function(key, tmparticle) {
						$('#block-1002915-lnp-most-popular-list').append('<li class=""><a href="'+tmparticle.url+'?utm_source=general&utm_medium=list&utm_campaign=People%20Are%20Reading'+'">'+tmparticle.title+'<\/a><\/li>');
						
					});
					/* need to reset ajax */
					$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);	
				})
				.fail(function(errStatus) {
					console.log (errStatus);
					/* need to reset ajax */
					$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);	
				});
			}
		} else {
			
				$.getJSON('https://lancasteronline.com/search/?f=json&t=article&&l=5&sort=date&c[]=news/local&k=&b=&sd=desc&d1=24%20hours%20ago&xd=1',
			function(lnpsearchlist, status) {
			})
			.done(function(lnpsearchlist) {
				$.each(lnpsearchlist.items, function(key, tmparticle) {
					$('#block-1002915-lnp-most-popular-list').append('<li class=""><a href="'+tmparticle.url+'?utm_source=general&utm_medium=list&utm_campaign=People%20Are%20Reading'+'">'+tmparticle.title+'<\/a><\/li>');
				});
				/* need to reset ajax */
				$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);	
			})
			.fail(function(errStatus) {
				console.log (errStatus);
				/* need to reset ajax */
				$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);	
			});
		}
		/* need to reset ajax */
		$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);
	})
	.fail(function(errStatus) {
		
		$.getJSON('https://lancasteronline.com/search/?f=json&t=article&&l=5&sort=date&c[]=news/local&k=&b=&sd=desc&d1=24%20hours%20ago&xd=1',
		function(lnpsearchlist, status) {
		})
		.done(function(lnpsearchlist) {
			$.each(lnpsearchlist.items, function(key, tmparticle) {
				$('#block-1002915-lnp-most-popular-list').append('<li class=""><a href="'+tmparticle.url+'?utm_source=general&utm_medium=list&utm_campaign=People%20Are%20Reading'+'">'+tmparticle.title+'<\/a><\/li>');
			});
			/* need to reset ajax */
			$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);	
		})
		.fail(function(errStatus) {
			console.log (errStatus);
			/* need to reset ajax */
			$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);	
		});
		console.log (errStatus);
		/* need to reset ajax */
		$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);
	});
});
           </script>

            </ul>

                  Beware partisan websites masquerading as news sites. Newspapers such as LNP | LancasterOnline are far more reliable. [editorial]

       var allplans = [];
    var parselyPlan = null;

    var parselySubPlan = null;
    var parselyLoggedIn = '';
    
    function setSyncDFPCookie(syncdfpcname,syncdfpcvalue,syncdfpexdays) {
	var syncdfpd = new Date();
	syncdfpd.setTime(syncdfpd.getTime() + (syncdfpexdays*24*60*60*1000));
	var syncdfpexpires = "expires=" + syncdfpd.toGMTString();
	document.cookie = syncdfpcname + "=" + syncdfpcvalue + ";" + syncdfpexpires + ";path=/";
    }
	var syncParselyLogin = function(callback) {
		sdkSync.getLoginStatus(function (data) {
		
			if (data.loggedIn == true) {
				parselyLoggedIn = true;
			}
			sdkSync.getSubscriberStatus(function (data) {
				$.each(data.planList, function(i, planList) {
					if (planList.active) {
						allplans.push(planList.planCode);
					}
				});
				if ((allplans.indexOf("LOLSPORTS") > -1) || (allplans.indexOf("QSPORTS") > -1) ||
                                    (allplans.indexOf("LOLOBITS") > -1) || (allplans.indexOf("QOBITS") > -1) ||
                                    (allplans.indexOf("LOLPOWER") > -1) || (allplans.indexOf("QPOWER") > -1)) {
					var syncmsg = document.createElement('style')
					syncmsg.innerHTML = ".sdmsg{display:none !important;} .somsg{display:block !important;}";
					document.body.appendChild(syncmsg);
				} else {
					var syncmsg = document.createElement('style')
					syncmsg.innerHTML = ".somsg{display:none !important;} .sdmsg{display:block !important;}";
					document.body.appendChild(syncmsg);
				};
                
				callback();
			}, function (errStatus) {
				console.log (errStatus);
				callback();
			}); 
		}, function (errStatus) {
			console.log (errStatus);
			callback();			
		});
	};

        var isLNPSubscriber;
	syncParselyLogin(verifyParselyPlan);
});

function verifyParselyPlan() {
	if (allplans.length > 0) {
	
		/* need to override syncSDK ajaxSetup */
		$.cachedAjaxSetup = $.extend(true, {}, $.ajaxSetup());
		$.ajaxSetup({
			beforeSend: function (xhr) {    
			}
		});
                $.getJSON('https://dagobah.lancasteronline.com/archive/index.php/parsely/'+allplans, function(response, status) {
		})
		.done(function(response) {
			$.getJSON('https://dagobah.lancasteronline.com/archive/index.php/syncdfp/'+allplans, function(dfpresponse, status) {
			})
			.done(function(dfpresponse) {
				dfptargets = dfpresponse.response.plan.split(',');
				setSyncDFPCookie('_syncdfp',dfptargets,1);
			})
			.fail(function() {
				if (parselyLoggedIn) {
					setSyncDFPCookie('_syncdfp','registered',1);
				}
			});
			if (response.response.plan != false) {
				parselyPlan = response.response.plan;
                                parselyDayPass = response.response.daypass;
                                parselyOtherSub = response.response.othersub;
                                if (parselyDayPass == 'day') {
                                    parselySubPlan = parselyDayPass;
                                } else if (parselyOtherSub == 'other') {
                                    parselySubPlan = parselyOtherSub;
                                }
				
                                dataLayer.push({'isSubscriber': 'yes'});
                                isLNPSubscriber = 'yes';
                                dataLayer.push({'isLoggedIn': 'yes'});
                               
			} else if (parselyLoggedIn) {
				parselyPlan = 'registered';
                                parselyDayPass = response.response.daypass;
                                parselyOtherSub = response.response.othersub;
                                if (parselyDayPass == 'day') {
                                    parselySubPlan = parselyDayPass;
                                } else if (parselyOtherSub == 'other') {
                                    parselySubPlan = parselyOtherSub;
                                }
				setSyncDFPCookie('_syncdfp','registered',1);

                                dataLayer.push({'isSubscriber': 'no'});
                                isLNPSubscriber = 'no';
                                dataLayer.push({'isLoggedIn': 'yes'});
				
			}
			
			/* need to reset ajax */
    		$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);
    			
			//console.log ('parselyplan='+parselyPlan);
			(function(w) {
				w.PARSELY = {
					autotrack: false,
					onReady: function() {
						PARSELY.updateDefaults({
							data: {
								plan: parselyPlan,
                                                                subplan: parselySubPlan
							}
						});
						PARSELY.beacon.trackPageView();
					}
				};
			})(window);
			(function(s, p, d) {
			  var h=d.location.protocol, i=p+"-"+s,
				  e=d.getElementById(i), r=d.getElementById(p+"-root"),
				  u=h==="https:"?"d1z2jf7jlzjs58.cloudfront.net"
				  :"static."+p+".com";
			  if (e) return;
			  e = d.createElement(s); e.id = i; e.async = true;
			  e.src = h+"//"+u+"/p.js"; r.appendChild(e);
			})("script", "parsely", document);
		})
		.fail(function(errStatus) {
			console.log (errStatus);
			/* need to reset ajax */
			$.ajaxSetup($.cachedAjaxSetup);
    			
			if (parselyLoggedIn) {
				parselyPlan = 'registered';
				setSyncDFPCookie('_syncdfp','registered',1);

				
                                dataLayer.push({'isSubscriber': 'no'});
                                isLNPSubscriber = 'no';
                                isLNPSubscriber = 'no';
                                dataLayer.push({'isLoggedIn': 'yes'});
 
			}
			//console.log ('parselyplan='+parselyPlan);
			(function(w) {
				w.PARSELY = {
					autotrack: false,
					onReady: function() {
						PARSELY.updateDefaults({
							data: {
								plan: parselyPlan,
                                                                subplan: parselySubPlan
							}
						});
						PARSELY.beacon.trackPageView();
					}
				};
			})(window);

				  u=h==="https:"?"d1z2jf7jlzjs58.cloudfront.net"
				  :"static."+p+".com";

			  e = d.createElement(s); e.id = i; e.async = true;
			  e.src = h+"//"+u+"/p.js"; r.appendChild(e);
			})("script", "parsely", document);
		});
	} else {
		if (parselyLoggedIn) {
			parselyPlan = 'registered';
                        setSyncDFPCookie('_syncdfp','registered',1);
			
                        dataLayer.push({'isSubscriber': 'no'});
                        isLNPSubscriber = 'no';
                        dataLayer.push({'isLoggedIn': 'yes'});
			
		} else {
                        dataLayer.push({'isSubscriber': 'no'});
                        isLNPSubscriber = 'no';
                        dataLayer.push({'isLoggedIn': 'no'});
                }
                
		//console.log ('parselyplan='+parselyPlan);
		(function(w) {
			w.PARSELY = {
				autotrack: false,
				onReady: function() {
					PARSELY.updateDefaults({
						data: {
							plan: parselyPlan,
                                                        subplan: parselySubPlan

       // Set to false if opt-in required
var trackByDefault = true;

function acEnableTracking() {
	var expiration = new Date(new Date().getTime() + 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 30);
	document.cookie = "ac_enable_tracking=1; expires= " + expiration + "; path=/";
	acTrackVisit();
}

function acTrackVisit() {
	var trackcmp_email = '';
	var trackcmp = document.createElement("script");
	trackcmp.async = true;
	trackcmp.type = 'text/javascript';

   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

   /*<![CDATA[*/ 
                __tnt.googleEvent = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'gaTriggerEvent',
                        'gaEventCategory': obj.category,
                        'gaEventAction': obj.action,
                        'gaEventLabel': obj.label,
                        'gaEventValue': obj.value
                    });
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.trigger',
                             'tncms.event.trigger.category': obj.category,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.action': obj.action,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.label': obj.label, 
                             'tncms.event.trigger.value': obj.value
                    });
                }
                __tnt.googleSocial = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'socialEvent',
                        'socialNetwork': obj.network,
                        'socialAction': obj.socialAction,
                        'socialTarget': obj.url
                    });

                        'event': 'tncms.event.social',
                            'tncms.event.social.network': obj.network,
                            'tncms.event.social.action': obj.socialAction,
                            'tncms.event.social.target': obj.url
                    });
                }

                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.title': obj.title
                    });
                } /*]]>*/
